# Skills-Repository
Certainly! Below is a README file with links and descriptions for each of the academic and tutoring subjects listed. This README provides brief descriptions and links to relevant websites where users can learn more about each subject.

---

# Academic and Tutoring Resources

## Academic Achievement
- **Description**: Enhance your academic performance and reach your educational goals.
- **Learn More**: [Khan Academy](https://www.khanacademy.org) - Free educational resources across a wide range of subjects.

## Academic Advising
- **Description**: Get guidance on course selection, career paths, and academic planning.
- **Learn More**: [NACADA](https://www.nacada.ksu.edu) - Resources and support for academic advising.

## Accounting Tutoring
- **Description**: Improve your understanding of accounting principles and practices.
- **Learn More**: [AccountingCoach](https://www.accountingcoach.com) - Free online tutorials and articles.

## Algebra Tutoring
- **Description**: Master algebra concepts and solve complex equations with ease.
- **Learn More**: [Khan Academy](https://www.khanacademy.org/math/algebra) - Comprehensive algebra lessons and practice exercises.

## Calculus Tutoring
- **Description**: Learn the fundamentals of calculus, including derivatives and integrals.
- **Learn More**: [Paul's Online Math Notes](http://tutorial.math.lamar.edu) - Detailed calculus tutorials and notes.

## Chemistry Tutoring
- **Description**: Understand chemical reactions, periodic table, and more in chemistry.
- **Learn More**: [ChemCollective](http://chemcollective.org) - Virtual labs and chemistry resources.

## Chinese Tutoring
- **Description**: Learn to read, write, and speak Chinese with expert guidance.
- **Learn More**: [ChinesePod](https://www.chinesepod.com) - Online Mandarin Chinese lessons and resources.

## Coding Lesson
- **Description**: Gain coding skills in various programming languages and technologies.
- **Learn More**: [Codecademy](https://www.codecademy.com) - Interactive coding lessons and projects.

## College Tutoring
- **Description**: Receive support in various subjects to excel in your college courses.
- **Learn More**: [Chegg Tutors](https://www.chegg.com/tutors) - On-demand tutoring for college subjects.

## Computer Science Tutoring
- **Description**: Learn computer science concepts, from algorithms to data structures.
- **Learn More**: [Coursera](https://www.coursera.org) - Online courses in computer science from top universities.

## Education Consulting
- **Description**: Get expert advice on educational planning and school selection.

## English Teaching

# Telecommunications Resources

## Access Point Identification
- **Description**: Identify and manage wireless access points within a network.
- **Learn More**: [NetSpot](https://www.netspotapp.com) - Wireless network survey app for access point identification.

## Active Site Survey
- **Description**: Conduct surveys to assess the performance and coverage of a wireless network.
- **Learn More**: [Ekahau](https://www.ekahau.com) - Tools for professional Wi-Fi site surveys.

## Aerial Technical Site Survey
- **Description**: Use aerial methods to survey and map site locations and conditions.
- **Learn More**: [DroneDeploy](https://www.dronedeploy.com) - Drone software for aerial surveys and site mapping.

## Base Station Equipment Management
- **Description**: Manage and maintain the equipment used at base stations in a network.
- **Learn More**: [Huawei](https://www.huawei.com) - Solutions for base station management.

## Blueprint Calibration
- **Description**: Adjust and calibrate blueprints for accurate network planning.
- **Learn More**: [AutoCAD](https://www.autodesk.com/products/autocad/overview) - Software for precision blueprint calibration.

## Discord
- **Description**: Utilize Discord for team communication and collaboration on telecommunications projects.
- **Learn More**: [Discord](https://discord.com) - Chat and collaboration platform for teams.

## Floorplan Blueprinting
- **Description**: Create and modify floorplans for accurate network installation and coverage.
- **Learn More**: [Floorplanner](https://www.floorplanner.com) - Online tool for creating and editing floorplans.

## HetNet Access Point Installation
- **Description**: Install heterogeneous network (HetNet) access points for improved coverage.
- **Learn More**: [Small Cell Forum](https://www.smallcellforum.org) - Resources on HetNet and small cell deployment.

## Hidden Wireless Network Detection
- **Description**: Detect and identify hidden wireless networks within an area.
- **Learn More**: [Wireshark](https://www.wireshark.org) - Network protocol analyzer for detecting hidden networks.

## Live Survey
- **Description**: Conduct real-time surveys to assess network performance and coverage.
- **Learn More**: [iBwave](https://www.ibwave.com) - Solutions for live network surveys and analysis.

## Passive Site Survey
- **Description**: Perform surveys to collect data on existing network performance without active transmissions.
- **Learn More**: [NetSpot](https://www.netspotapp.com) - Passive site survey tools for Wi-Fi networks.

## Physical Site Survey
- **Description**: Conduct on-site surveys to evaluate physical conditions and infrastructure for network installation.
- **Learn More**: [Viavi Solutions](https://www.viavisolutions.com) - Tools and resources for physical site surveys.

## PnP BTS Configuration
- **Description**: Configure Plug and Play base transceiver stations (BTS) for network deployment.
- **Learn More**: [Ericsson](https://www.ericsson.com) - Resources and solutions for BTS configuration.

## Pre-inspection Visits
- **Description**: Conduct pre-inspection visits to evaluate site conditions before network deployment.
- **Learn More**: [Field Nation](https://www.fieldnation.com) - Platform for managing pre-inspection visits and field services.

## Predictive Site Survey
- **Description**: Use predictive modeling to assess network performance and coverage before deployment.
- **Learn More**: [Ekahau](https://www.ekahau.com) - Tools for predictive Wi-Fi site surveys.

## Radio Access Network Commissioning
- **Description**: Commission and integrate radio access network (RAN) components.
- **Learn More**: [Nokia](https://www.nokia.com) - Solutions for RAN commissioning and integration.

## RAN Call Testing
- **Description**: Perform call testing to evaluate the performance of radio access networks.
- **Learn More**: [Keysight](https://www.keysight.com) - Tools for RAN call testing and analysis.

## RAN NMS Integration
- **Description**: Integrate radio access networks with network management systems (NMS).
- **Learn More**: [Cisco](https://www.cisco.com) - Solutions for RAN and NMS integration.

## Remote Quality Audit
- **Description**: Conduct remote audits to assess network quality and performance.
- **Learn More**: [Spirent](https://www.spirent.com) - Tools for remote network quality audits.

## RF Manual Site Survey
- **Description**: Perform manual surveys to evaluate radio frequency (RF) conditions and performance.
- **Learn More**: [RF Venue](https://www.rfvenue.com) - Resources and tools for RF site surveys.

## RF Site Survey
- **Description**: Assess RF conditions and plan network coverage through site surveys.
- **Learn More**: [Ekahau](https://www.ekahau.com) - RF site survey tools and solutions.

## Rogue Access Point Detection
- **Description**: Detect unauthorized access points in a wireless network.
- **Learn More**: [AirMagnet](https://www.netscout.com/product/airmagnet-wifi-analyzer) - Tools for rogue access point detection.

## Signal Propagation Assessment
- **Description**: Evaluate how signals propagate through different environments for optimal coverage.
- **Learn More**: [CommScope](https://www.commscope.com) - Solutions for signal propagation and network planning.

## Small Cell Deployment
- **Description**: Deploy small cells to enhance network coverage and capacity.
- **Learn More**: [Small Cell Forum](https://www.smallcellforum.org) - Resources for small cell deployment.

## TeamViewer
- **Description**: Use TeamViewer for remote access and support in telecommunications projects.
- **Learn More**: [TeamViewer](https://www.teamviewer.com) - Remote support and access solutions.

## Technical Site Audit
- **Description**: Conduct technical audits to ensure site compliance with network standards.
- **Learn More**: [Viavi Solutions](https://www.viavisolutions.com) - Tools for technical site audits.

## Technical Site Survey
- **Description**: Perform comprehensive surveys to evaluate technical requirements and conditions for network deployment.
- **Learn More**: [Ekahau](https://www.ekahau.com) - Comprehensive tools for technical site surveys.

## Walking Path Analysis
- **Description**: Analyze walking paths to optimize network coverage and performance.
- **Learn More**: [Esri](https://www.esri.com) - GIS solutions for walking path analysis and planning.

## Wireless Access Point Installation
- **Description**: Install wireless access points for optimal network coverage and performance.
- **Learn More**: [Ubiquiti](https://www.ui.com) - Solutions and guides for wireless access point installation.

## Wireless Capacity Analysis
- **Description**: Assess and plan for wireless network capacity to meet user demand.
- **Learn More**: [Cisco](https://www.cisco.com) - Tools for wireless capacity analysis and planning.

## Wireless Coverage Assessment
- **Description**: Evaluate and improve wireless network coverage in various environments.
- **Learn More**: [NetSpot](https://www.netspotapp.com) - Tools for wireless coverage assessment.

## Wireless Network Risk Analysis & Reduction
- **Description**: Analyze risks in wireless networks and implement measures to reduce them.
- **Learn More**: [Cisco](https://www.cisco.com) - Solutions for wireless network risk analysis and management.

## Wireless Network Security Analysis
- **Description**: Assess the security of wireless networks and identify vulnerabilities.
- **Learn More**: [Wireshark](https://www.wireshark.org) - Network analysis tools for security assessments.

## Wireless Security Audit
- **Description**: Conduct audits to ensure wireless network security and compliance.
- **Learn More**: [AirMagnet](https://www.netscout.com/product/airmagnet-wifi-analyzer) - Tools for wireless security audits.

## Wireless Site Survey
- **Description**: Perform comprehensive surveys to plan and optimize wireless network deployment.
- **Learn More**: [Ekahau](https://www.ekahau.com) - Professional tools for wireless site surveys.

## Business, Accounting, Human Resources & Legal

### A/R Analysis

- **Learn More**: [HubSpot](https://blog.hubspot.com/service/account-management) - Comprehensive guide on account management.

### Account Payables Management

### Account Receivables Management

### Engineering & Science Skills Overview

#### 802.11
- **Description**: Standard for wireless networking (WiFi) technology.
- **Learn More**: [IEEE 802.11](https://standards.ieee.org/802_11.html)

#### A&P
- **Description**: Airframe and Powerplant certification for aviation maintenance technicians.
- **Learn More**: [FAA A&P Certification](https://www.faa.gov)

#### A1 Assessor
- **Description**: Qualification for assessing vocational competencies.
- **Learn More**: [City & Guilds A1 Assessor](https://www.cityandguilds.com)

#### AAUS Scientific Diver
- **Description**: Certification for scientific diving practices.
- **Learn More**: [AAUS Scientific Diver](https://www.aaus.org)

#### ABC Analysis
- **Description**: Inventory categorization technique based on consumption value.
- **Learn More**: [Investopedia ABC Analysis](https://www.investopedia.com)

#### AC Drives
- **Description**: Variable frequency drives used to control AC motor speed and torque.
- **Learn More**: [AutomationDirect](https://www.automationdirect.com)

#### Accelerator Physics
- **Description**: Study of the physics of particle accelerators.
- **Learn More**: [CERN](https://home.cern)

#### Acoustical Engineering
- **Description**: Engineering discipline dealing with sound and vibration.
- **Learn More**: [Acoustical Society of America](https://acousticalsociety.org)

- **Description**: Engineering discipline focused on aircraft design and development.
- **Learn More**: [AIAA](https://www.aiaa.org)

#### Aerospace Engineering
- **Description**: Broader field including both aeronautical and astronautical engineering.
- **Learn More**: [NASA](https://www.nasa.gov)

- **Description**: Science and technology of producing and using plants for food, fuel, fiber, and land reclamation.
- **Learn More**: [American Society of Agronomy](https://www.agronomy.org)

- **Learn More**: [Tagline Creation](https://www.wordstream.com/blog/ws/2020/08/17/slogan-examples)

#### Technical Documentation
- **Description**: Writing manuals and documentation for technical products and processes.
- **Learn More**: [Technical Documentation](https://www.stc.org/)

#### Technical Writing
- **Description**: Writing about technical subjects in a clear and concise manner.
- **Learn More**: [Technical Writing](https://www.stc.org/)

#### Test Plan Writing
- **Description**: Writing plans for testing software and systems.
- **Learn More**: [Test Plan Writing](https://www.guru99.com/test-plan.html)

#### Test Strategy Writing
- **Description**: Writing strategies for systematic testing approaches.
- **Learn More**: [Test Strategy Writing](https://www.softwaretestinghelp.com/)

#### Translation
- **Description**: Converting text from one language to another.
- **Learn More**: [Translation Services](https://www.proz.com/)

#### Travel Writing
- **Description**: Writing about travel destinations, experiences, and tips.
- **Learn More**: [Travel Writing](https://www.travelwriters.com/)

#### Web Page Writer
- **Description**: Writing content specifically for web pages.
- **Learn More**: [Web Page Writing](https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/web-content)

#### White Paper
- **Description**: Writing authoritative reports on complex issues.
- **Learn More**: [White Paper Writing](https://www.wordstream.com/blog/ws/2018/03/19/white-paper)

#### WIKI
- **Description**: Writing and editing content for wiki platforms.
- **Learn More**: [Wikis](https://www.wikispaces.com/)

#### Wikipedia
- **Description**: Contributing to or utilizing Wikipedia for information.
- **Learn More**: [Wikipedia](https://www.wikipedia.org/)

#### Word Processing
- **Description**: Creating, formatting, and editing documents using word processing software.
- **Learn More**: [Word Processing](https://www.microsoft.com

/en-us/microsoft-365/word)

#### Writing
- **Description**: General category encompassing all forms of written communication.
- **Learn More**: [Writing](https://www.writersdigest.com/)
